# <a name="azure-resource-manager-resource-provider-operations"></a><span data-ttu-id="82250-103">Operazioni di provider di risorse con Azure Resource Manager</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82250-103">Azure Resource Manager Resource Provider operations</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="82250-104">Questo documento elenca le operazioni disponibili per ciascun provider di risorse Microsoft Azure Resource Manager.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82250-104">This document lists the operations available for each Microsoft Azure Resource Manager resource provider.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82250-105">Tali operazioni possono essere utilizzate nei ruoli personalizzati per fornire autorizzazioni RBAC (controllo degli accessi in base al ruolo) granulari alle risorse di Azure.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82250-105">These can be used in custom roles to provide granular Role-Based Access Control (RBAC) permissions to resources in Azure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82250-106">L’elenco qui fornito non è da ritenersi completo e le operazioni potrebbero essere aggiunte o rimosse man mano che il provider viene aggiornato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82250-106">Please note this is not a comprehensive list and operations may be added or removed as each provider is updated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82250-107">Le stringhe di operazione seguono il formato di `Microsoft.<ProviderName>/<ChildResourceType>/<action>`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82250-107">Operation strings follow the format of `Microsoft.<ProviderName>/<ChildResourceType>/<action>`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82250-108">Per un elenco completo e aggiornato delle operazioni dei provider di risorse di Azure utilizzare `Get-AzureRmProviderOperation` (in PowerShell) o `azure provider operations show` (in Azure CLI).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82250-108">For a comprehensive and current list please use `Get-AzureRmProviderOperation` (in PowerShell) or `azure provider operations show` (in Azure CLI) to list operations of Azure resource providers.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="82250-2800">Operazione</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82250-2800">Operation</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="82250-2801">Descrizione</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82250-2801">Description</span></span> |
